\alnum{a} (kaMpUyxTarf) $1024$ (aMdare $2^{10}$) beYTugaLu athavA saDilavAgi $1000$ beYTugaLu.

\bentry
\word{kangaroo-rat}
\pron{kAYxMgarUrAYxTf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{%

kangaroo}.}

\word[keel(3)]{keel}
\pron{kiVlf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{(\birx) (\ca) 
\num{1} kalilxdadxla haDagu; (iMgelxMDinalilx) TeYnf nadi \mo vugaLa meVle kalilxdadxla haDagugaLige kalilxdadxlanunx sAgisuva capapxTe taLada haDagu. 
\num{2} (iMtaha haDaginalilx heVruva) kalilxdadxla heVru.}

\bentry

\pron{kiVnf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{%

\num{4} (noVvu, yAtane, \mo vugaLa \vi) kaTuvAda; tiVvarxvAda; tALalAgada; asahaniVya; sahisalAgada. 
\num{5} (vayxkitx, bayake, Asakitx, \mo vugaLa \vi) utusxka; tavakapaDuva; tiVvArxsakitxya; utAsxhashAli; utAsxhaBarita: \eng{keen sportsman} utAsxhashAliyAda kirxVDApaTu. 
\num{6} (kaNuNx, daqSiTx, vAsanAshakitx, \mo vugaLa \vi) curukAda; tiVkaSxNXvAda; sUkaSxmXvAda. 
\num{7} curukubudidhxya; kushAgarxbudidhxya; sUkaSxmXbudidhxyuLaLx; tiVkaSxNXmatiyAda. 
\num{8} (\birx) (beleya \vi) peYpoVTiya; (peYpoVTiya kAraNadiMdAgi) bahaLa agagxvAda.

\bentry
\word[keep(1)]{keep}
\pron{kiVpf}
\gl{\kirx} (\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{kept} \ucAcx\ kepfTx).

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kAyide, vAgAdxna, tananxlilxTaTx naMbike, kwlu, karAru, nishicxta BeVTi, \mo vanunx)
pAlisu; anusarisu; naDesu; gwravisu: \eng{keep one's word} mAtina parxkAra naDe. 
\num{2} (hababx, varxta, \mo vanunx) mADu; naDesu; neraveVrisu; Acarisu.
\num{3} (vayxkitx, dugaR, paTaTxNa, phuTfbAlina goVlu, \mo vanunx)
kAyu; kApADu; rakiSxsu; \eng{God keep you} deVvaru ninanxnunx
rakiSxsali.
\num{4} noVDiko; (oMdara) javAbAdxrivahisu: \eng{keep children} makakxLanunx noVDiko.
\num{5} (vashadalilxruva vasutxvanunx) irisiko; iTuTxko: \eng{you may keep
the change} cilalxreyanunx (vApAsu mADabeVkAgilalxde) niVneV iTuTxko.
\num{6} (mane \mo vanunx) cenAnxgi, cokakxTavAgi, sariyAda sithxtiyalilx -- iTuTxko. 
\num{7} (aMgaDi \mo vanunx) sariyAgi nivaRhisu, iTuTxko; naDesikoMDu
hoVgu. 
\num{8} (dinacari, lekAkxcArada pusatxka, \mo vanunx vivaragaLanenxlalx dAKalu mADi) karxmavAgi irisu, iDu, iTiTxru. 
\num{9} (kuTuMba, tAnu, \mo vanunx) salahu; hore; noVDiko; poVSisu; jiVvanoVpAya odagisi iTuTxko, iTuTxkoMDiru.
\num{10} (hasugaLu, jeVnuhuLu, \mo vanunx) sAku; sAki iTuTxko: \eng{keep bees}
jeVnu sAku. 
\num{11} (obAbxkeyanunx upaBoVgakAkxgi. upapatinxyanAnxgi, raKAvf Agi) iTuTxkoMDiru; maDagikoMDiru. 
\num{12} (sarakanunx, mAlanunx) mArATakekx sadA -- hoMdiru. iTiTxru: \eng{do you keep buttons} niVvu guMDigaLanunx (mArATakekx) iTiTxdidxVrA? 
\num{13} uLisiTuTxkoMDiru; kApADiTuTxkoMDiru; asitxtavxdalilxTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{14} (vayxkitxyanunx sereyalilx, baMdhanadalilx) iTiTxru; hiDidiTiTxru. 
\num{15} takakx yA sUcita sithxtiyalilx iTuTxkoMDiru: \eng{keep them happy} avaranunx saMtoVSavAgiTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{16} (vayxkitxyanunx, tananxnenxV, yAvudeV kelasavanunx mADadaMte) taDe; niroVdhisu; taDehiDi: \eng{will keep you
from going too fast} atiyAda veVgadalilx hoVgadaMte ninanxnunx taDeyutAtxne.
\num{17} (vayxkitxyanunx seremaneyalilx \mo\ kaDe) hiDidiDu; taDedu nililxsu:
\eng{what kept you so long?} ninanxnunx iSuTx hotutx yAvudu taDeditutx,
hiDidiTiTxtutx? 
\num{18} (yAvudeV vasutxvanunx, muMdina upayoVgakAkxgi)
uLisiTiTxru; baLasade iTiTxru; kAdirisu; kAdiDu: \eng{keep it for tomorrow}
nALege uLisiTiTxru. 
\hypertarget{keep(19)}{}
\num{19} mucicxTiTxru; bacicxTiTxru; goVpayxvAgi, guTATxgi, rahasayxvAgi -- iTiTxru: \eng{keep one's \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{counsel(1) nuga(2)}{${}^1$counsel}.} tananx iMgitavanunx 
goVpayxvAgiDu; aBipArxyavanunx biTuTx koDadiru; bAyi biDadiru; mwnavAgiru.
\num{20} (dAri, mADutitxruva kelasa, \mo vanunx) anusarisutAtx hoVgu; biDade mADutAtx hoVgu; hiDidiru; biDadiru: \eng{he keeps his own course} avanu tananx dAriyanenxV hiDiyutAtxne.
\num{21} (hAsige, koThaDi, mane, \mo vanunx) biTuTx baradiru; (hAsige \mo
vugaLalelxV) iru. 
\num{22} (parxtiBaTaneyanunx lekikxsade, kudureya meVle,
keSxVtarx, raMgasathxLa, niMta nele, itAyxdiyalilx) kadaladiru; BadarxvAgiru;
tananx sAthxna biDadiru, badalAyisadiru. 
\num{23} (oMdu niyatavAda sathxLadalilx, jAgadalilx) iDu; irisu:
\eng{knives are kept in this drawer} I seLeKAneyalilx cAkugaLanunx
iTiTxde.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (maneyoLageV) iru: \eng{keep indoors} maneyoLageV iru. 
\num{2} (\AmA, \kanmu\ keVMbirxjf \vivi) iru; vAsisu:
\eng{where do you keep?} niVnu elilx ididxVye? elilx vAsavAgididxVye?
\num{3} (yAvudeV hesarisida sithxtiyalilx) iru: \eng{keep in good health}
AroVgayxvaMtanAgiru. \eng{keep cool} shAMtanAgiru. 
\num{4} (nideRVshisida, hesarisida, dikukx, dAri, kAyaR, \mo vugaLalilx) sAgiru; muMduvariyutitxru:
\eng{keep straight on for two miles} inUnx eraDu meYli neVravAgi muMduvariyutitxru. \eng{she keeps giggling} Ake kisakisane nagutatxleV irutAtxLe.
\num{5} (AhAra padAthaR, \mo vugaLa \vi) hadageDadiru; haLasadiru; keDadiru.

\num{41} \eng{keep up with} sarisamanAgiru; samavAgi hejejx hAku; adeV veVga hoMdiru. 
\hyperdef{K}{keep(1) nuga(42)}{}

nereyavarige (sAmAjikavAgi) sarisamanAgi bALu; sariVkaroMdige parxtiSeThx uLisiko.

\num{4} (jAhiVrAtige parxtiyAgi baruva utatxragaLanunx gurutisalu sahAyavAguvaMte, niyatakAlikada jAhiVrAtige) okakxNe -- bare, racisu; padagaLanunx odagisu.
\num{5} (gAre \mo vu aMTuvaMte mADalu goVDe \mo vugaLa) meVlemx\kern 2ptYyanunx -- oraTugoLisu, oraTu mADu. 
\num{6} (kiVli padadiMda gUDhalipi baraha
\mo vanunx) BeVdisu; athaRvAguvaMte mADu; atheYRsu; vivarisu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga} 
\dictmeaning{\eng{key up} (\rUpa)

\mo vugaLige) utetxVjisu; hurupugoLisu.

nidiRSaTx guNa yA tiVvarxte niVDu; (avanunx beVkAda maTaTxkekx) Erisu.

\alnum{d} (bele, beVDike, parxyatanx, \mo vanunx)
hecicxsu; Erisu.

\bentry

\bentry

{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kAliniMda) yAvudanenxV ode; latetxkoDu: \eng{kicked him} avananunx odeda. 
\num{2} odedodedu muMdUDu; odeyutAtx taLuLx. 
\num{3} (phuTfbAlf) odetadiMda goVlf hoDe. 
\num{4} (joVrAgi matutx tirasAkxradiMda) odudx dUDu: \eng{kick him out} avananunx ododxVDisu. \eng{kicked him downstairs} avananunx odudx mahaDiyiMda keLakekx taLiLxde. 
\num{5} (\ashi) (aBAyxsa yA cALiyanunx) tore; biDu; tayxjisu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} ode; latetxkoDu. 
\num{2} (sUcane, salahe, tanage doreta anAdara, \mo vugaLa \vi)
kirikiri, asamAdhAna, asaMtoVSa -- toVru: \eng{kick at the proposal}
salaheya viSayadalilx asamAdhAna toVru. \eng{kick against the
treatment} tananxnunx naDesikoMDa, tanonxDane naDedukoMDa, riVtiya
viSayadalilx kirikiri paDu, asaMtoVSa paDu.
\num{3} (bwlf mADida kirxkeTf ceMDina \vi) nelakekx taguli puTaveVLu; neladiMda nege.}} 

\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{alive(2) pagu(1)}{${}^2$alive} and kicking} caTuvaTikeyiMda kUDi.

\alnum{a} (joVDu \mo vanunx) kAlodari bisADu. 

\alnum{b} (ceMDanunx odedu) phuTfbAlf ATa pArxraMBisu. 

\alnum{c} (\AmA) (yAvudanenxV) AraMBisu; shuru mADu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} \eng{kick about (\engit{or} around)} 

\alnum{a} (obabxnanunx) oraToraTAgi yA tirasAkxradiMda kANu. 

\alnum{b} (viSayavanunx) aDADxdiDiDxyAgi caciRsu; karxmavilalxde, vayxvasethxyilalxde caciRsu. 

\alnum{c} (kelasavilalxde) alilx ililx aledADutitxru; ililxMdalilxge sututxtitxru. 

\alnum{d} baLakeyilalxdiru; baLasade bididxru. 

\alnum{e} beVDadAdxgiru; anapeVkiSxtavAgiru. 
\num{2} \eng{kick against the pricks} (tananx vataRneyiMda tanageV keDaku uMTAgutitxdadxrU adanunx lekikxsade nirathaRkavAda 
moMDutanadiMda) meVlinavarige edurubidudx toMdare hecicxsiko. 
\hyperdef{K}{kick(2) nuga(3)}{}
\num{3} \eng{kick a person upstairs} (birudu, meVlina padavi, \mo vanunx koTuTx)
obabxnanunx Erisi mUlege kUrisu; baDitx koTuTx niviRVyaRgoLisu. 
\num{4} \eng{kick one's \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{heel(1) nuga(9)}{${}^1$heels}} kAyuvaMtAgu; kAyutatx niMtiru: \eng{do not keep me hear kicking my heels} nAnu ililx sumamxne kAyutAtx niMtiruvaMte mADabeVDa. 
\num{5} \eng{kick over the \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{trace(3) pagu}{${}^3$traces}} tuMTATa mADu; avidheVyate toVrisu. 
\num{6} \eng{kick the \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bucket(1) nuga(2)}{${}^1$bucket}} (\ashi) kaMte oge; sAyu. 
\num{7} \eng{kick up}.
\num{8} \eng{\hyperlink{kicknuga9}{kick up a fuss}.= \hyperlink{kicknuga9}{\nuga($9$)}.}
\hypertarget{kicknuga9}{}
\num{9} \eng{kick up dust} 

\alnum{a} dhULebibxsu. 

\alnum{b} raMpa mADu; galATe, goMdala ebibxsu. 
\num{10} \eng{kick up its heels} (kudureya \vi) kirxVDeyalilx yA
ceVSeTxyalilx hiMgAletitx oge.}

\num{2} (roVga, duHKa, AGAta, madayxpAna, viSapAna, \mo vugaLa \vi) sAyisu; sAvanunxMTumADu; sAvanunx taru; sAvige kAraNavAgu.

\num{5} (BAvagaLu \mo vanunx) konegANisibiDu; aDagisi biDu; aLiyisu; dhavxMsa mADu.

\num{9} (lAnf Tenisf) (hiMdakekx kaLuhalAgadaMte, ceMDanunx) bArisu; hoDe.
\num{10} (phuTfbAlf) (muMdakekx calisadaMte ceMDanunx) taDedu biDu; nililxsibiDu; nishacxlagoLisu. 
\num{11} (pAliRmeMTinalilx, masUdeyanunx) hata mADibiDu; koMdu hAku; nipAta mADibiDu; pUtiRyAgi soVlisibiDu; tale etatxdaMte mADibiDu;
huTaTxDagisibiDu. 
\num{12} (husi dayeyiMda, dayA BArxMtiyiMda) keDakuMTumADu; hAniyuMTumADu. 
\num{13} pArxNigaLanunx koMdu mAMsa paDe. 
\num{14} (\AmA) tiVvarx yAtane koDu; bahaLa noVvuMTumADu: \eng{my feet are killing me} nananx kAlaDigaLu nananxnunx kolulxtitxve, nanage sahisalArada noVvu koDutitxve.
\num{15} (\AmA) (tiMDi tiVthaRgaLa \vi) dhavxMsa mADibiDu; (tiMdu, kuDidu)
KAli mADibiDu. 
\num{16} (honalu beLaku, yaMtarx, \mo vanunx) Arisu; nililxsu.
\num{17} (\AtAmx) 

\alnum{a} joVrAgi, gaTiTxyAgi -- nagu. 

\alnum{b} mitimiVri sharxmisi, vipariVta kelasa mADi baLalu: \eng{don't kill yourself lifting them all at once} oMdeV bArige avelalxvanUnx oTiTxge etitx susAtxgabeVDa, baLalabeVDa. 
\num{18} (\AmA) kaMpUyxTarf pheYlfniMda(oMdu sAlu, pAyxrA, \mo vanunx) -- tegeduhAku, kitutxhAku.}}

\bentry
\word[kind(1)]{kind}
\pron{keYMDf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} (sasayx, pArxNi, \mo vugaLa) buDakaTuTx; kula: \eng{human
kind} mAnava kula.  
\num{2} jAti; sAvxBAvika vagaR; \eng{rabbit kind} molada jAti. 
\num{3} (\kerxY) parxBuBoVjana saMsAkxradalilx viniyoVgisuva berxDuDx
yA veYnu.
\num{4} (heVLutitxruva viSaya kaTuTxniTATxdadadxlalx,
niSakxqqSaTxvAdadadxlalx, yA utepxrXVkeSxya mAtu, eMdu muMtAgi
sUcisuvalilx) EnoV oMdu bageya; oMdu -- namUneya, vidhada, terana,
tarahada: \eng{he is a kind of millionaire} 
avanu oMdu bageya lakASxdhipati. \eng{I felt a kind of compunction}
nanage EnoV oMdu bageya anutApa yA pashAcxtAtxpa uMTAyitu.  
\num{5} (\pArxparx) nisagaR, parxkaqti; nisagaRda -- karxma
vayxvasethx.  
\num{6} (vayxkitx \mo vakekx) sahajavAda -- mAgaR, riVti, savxBAva,
vidhAna: \eng{they act after their kind} tamamx tamamx sahaja riVtige
takakxMte avaru vatiRsutAtxre.  
\num{7} savxBAva; parxkaqti; guNa; lakaSxNa: \eng{they differ in kind
not merely in degree} avugaLigiruva vayxtAyxsa parxmANaBeVdavaSeTxV
alalx, guNaBeVda kUDa.}} 

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} \eng{law of kind} nisagaRda niyama. 
\num{2} \eng{kind of} (\AmA) savxlapxmaTiTxge: \eng{I had kind of
expected it} nAnu savxlapxmaTiTxge adanunx niriVkiSxsidedx. 
\hyperdef{K}{kind(1) pagu(3)}{}
\num{3} \eng{nothing of the kind} 

\alnum{a} A teranadalalxveV alalx. aMthadalalxveV alalx; hAgalalxveV alalx. 

\alnum{b} (nirAkaraNe sUcisuvalilx) KaMDita ilalx; bilfkulf ilalx;
sutarAM ilalx.  
\num{4} \eng{of a kind}

\alnum{a} (tirasAkxradalilx) yAvudoV oMdu bageya: \eng{we had coffee
of a kind} namage yAvudoV oMdu bageya kAphi sikikxtu; EnoV hesarige
kAphi enunxvudu sikikxtu.

\alnum{b} oMdu muKayxvAda aMshadalilx, riVtiyalilx -- oMdeV riVtiya, oMdeV terana, oMdeV bageya: \eng{they're two of a kind} avaribabxrU (oMdu muKayxvAda aMshadalilx) oMdeV bageyavaru. 
\num{5} \eng{of its kind} adeV vagaRda; adeV vagaRkekx seVrida; adara bageya parimitiyalilx; adaraMtha: \eng{good of its kind}
adaraMthadadxralilx oLeLxyadu. 
\num{6} \eng{one's own kind} tananxMthavaru; tananx samAnaru; tanonxDane aneVka samAnAMshagaLanunx hoMdiruvavaru; tananx sadaqsharu. 
\num{7} \eng{something of the kind} parxsakatx vasutxvina yA viSayada bageyadu yAvudoV oMdu; aMthadedxV oMdu; adeV tarahada oMdu.
\num{8} \eng{the kind of} bageya; terana; taraheya; vidhada: \eng{this is the kind of thing I meant} nananx manasisxnalilxdudxdu I bageya viSaya; nAnu heVLabayasidudx I vidhada viSaya. 
\num{9} \eng{this (\engit{or} these) kind of} (\AmA) I bageya: \eng{this kind of men annoy me} I bageya jana nanage kirikiri
uMTu mADutAtxre, siTuTx barisutAtxre. 
\num{10} \eng{what kind of} eMtaha; eMtha; yAva bageya, riVtiya,
jAtiya: \eng{what kind of tree is this?} idu yAva jAtiya mara?}}

\vi\ oLasaMcina ilalxveV nijavanunx mucicxruva dUru baMdidadxre aMtaha mokadadxmeyalilx parxveVshamADuva adhikAravuLaLx
koVTiRna adhikAri.

sidadhxpaDisuva, rAja, rANi yA avara parxtinidhiya saBeya muMde Oduva, videVshAMga matutx oLa ADaLitagaLa bagegx sakARrada 
niVtiyeVneMbudanUnx  adanunx kAyaRgata mADalu sakARravu keYgoLaLxliruva karxmagaLanUnx vivarisuva BASaNa.

\bentry

\pron{kipf janareVTarf}

\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (rakatx baMdhugaLa pirxVti, mamate, Apatxranunx kaMDAga uMTAguva saMtoVSa, pUjayxralilx Bakitx, ivugaLa kuruhAgi koDuva) mututx; cuMbana.
\num{2} (biliyaDfsxR) calisutitxruva ceMDugaLa parasapxra tAgu, sapxshaR, soVku(vike).

the kiss of death for a new work} hosa kaqtiyoMdakekx hitashaturxvAgiruva uguru becacxneya yA tusu mecicxkeya garxMtha vimasheRgaLu. 
\num{2} \eng{kiss of life} pArxNadAyaka mututx; jiVvadAni cuMbana; matetx badukisuva mututx; punarujijxVvaka cuMbana; peTuTx tiMda yA niVrinalilx muLugidadx vayxkitxge matetx sarAgavAgi usirADuvaMtAgalu avana bAyige tananx bAyiTuTx gALi Uduva kAyaRvidhAna. 
\num{3} \eng{kiss of peace} (parxBuBoVjana saMsAkxradalilx aikayxda kuruhAgi koDuva) dhAmiRka mututx; shAMti cuMbana (saMsAkxra).}}

\num{3} (biliyaDfsxR ATada ceMDina \vi) (beVroMdu ceMDanunx) mutitxDu; melalxge -- tAku, soVku; maqduvAgi -- sapxshiRsu, tagalu.}}

\num{4} \eng{kiss away} (kaMbani \mo vanunx) mutitxTuTx toDe, oresu, duHKavanunx hoVgalADisu, tolagisu. 
\num{5} \eng{kiss goodbye to} (\AmA) naSaTx opipxko. 
\num{6} \eng{kiss hands (of sovereign etc.)} (vidhivatAtxda vaMdaneya rUpadalilx, yA yAvudeV adhikArakekx neVmaka mADidadxkAkxgi kaqtajacnxteya rUpadalilx, dore \mo vara) keYge mutitxDu; hasatxcuMbana mADu. 
\num{7} \eng{kiss in-the-ring} cakarxcuMbanadATa; taruNa taruNiyaru cakArxkAravAgi ODutAtx, yAvaneV taruNanu
biVLisida karavasatxrXvanunx etitxkoMDa taruNiyu yA yAvaLeV taruNiyu biVLisida
karavasatxrXvanunx etitxkoMDa taruNanu, benanxTiTx hoVgi karavasatxrX biVLisida
vayxkitxyanunx mutitxDuva ATa. 
\num{8} \eng{kiss-me-quick} 

\alnum{a} taleya meVle tiVra hiMdakikxruva kiruToVpi. 

\alnum{b} \eng{= \hyperlink{kiss-curl}{kiss-curl}}. 
\num{9} \eng{kiss off} (\ashi) 

\alnum{a} tolagisu; tegeduhAku. 

\alnum{b} sAyu; maDi. 
\num{10} \eng{kiss one's hand to = \hyperlink{kiss(1)nuga}{${}^1$kiss {\rm \nuga}}}noVDi. 
\num{11} \eng{kiss the book}
(parxmANa mADuvalilx) beYbalalxnunx mutitxDu, beYbalalxnunx mutitxTuTx
parxmANa mADu. 
\num{12} \eng{kiss the dust} 

\alnum{a} (mAna mayARde toredu)
sharaNAgu; sharaNAgatanAgu; pAdAkArxMtanAgu; pAdadhULiyalilx horaLu.

sASATxMga parxNAma mADu.

\num{3} suligekoVra; durAseyiMda sikikxdadxnenxlalx doVcikoLuLxvavanu.

\num{5} (vANijayx \ashi) \eng{=
\hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{accommodation bill}{accommodation bill}.}

haDagina atayxMta meVlina hAyipaTagaLu.

\bentry
\word[knee(1)]{knee}
\pron{niV}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} (manuSayxna, pArxNiya) maMDi; moNakAlu; jAnu. 
\num{2} (kuLitiruva vayxkitxya) toDe; toDeya meVlABxga: \eng{hold the child on one's knee} maguvanunx toDeya meVle kUrisiko. 
\num{3} maMDiya, moNakAla -- sutitxna jAga. 
\num{4} maMDi; uDupinalilx maMDiyanunx mucucxva BAga. 
\num{5} maMDi; AkAradalilx yA sAthxnadalilx maMDiyanunx hoVluva yAvudeV vasutx, \kanmu\ oMdu koVnadalilx bagigxsida marada yA kabibxNada tuMDu, `gArxphf'nalilx kaDidAda tiruvu
\mo vu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{bend (\textit{or} bow) the knee} (\kanmu\ sharaNAgatiyalilx) maMDiyUru; maMDi bAgisu. 
\num{2} \eng{be on the knees of the Gods} deVvara keYyalilxru; deYvAyatatxvAgiru; Pala anishicxtavAgiru. 
\num{3} \eng{bring (person) to his or her knees} (vayxkitxyanunx) kAligeragisu; sharaNAgatananAnxgi mADu; kAlige biVLisu; kAlige biVLuva sithxtige taru. 
\num{4} \eng{give a knee to}

\alnum{a} (kusitxyalilx yA muSiTxkALagadalilx) jaTiTxyanunx (sULugaLa naDuve)
tananx maMDiya meVletitxkoMDu sudhArisikoLuLxvaMte mADu. 

\alnum{b} (kusitx \mo vugaLalilx obabxna) beMbaliganAgu; samathaRkanAgu. 

\num{5} \eng{on bended knee(s), on one's knee(s)} (beVDikoLuLxvalilx yA pArxthaRneyalilx, yA sharaNAgatanAdAga) maMDiyUri(koMDu).}

\bentry
\word[knock(1)]{knock}
\pron{nAkf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (sadAdxguvaMte balavAgi) hoDe; baDi; kuTuTx; gududx: \eng{he knocked the table thrice} avanu meVjanunx mUru bAri kuTiTxda. 
\num{2} (yAvudanenxV) hoDedu (adaralilx tUtu \mo vanunx) mADu: \eng{knock a hole in the wall} hoDedu goVDeyalilx tUtu mADu. 
\num{3} (\ashi) KaMDisu; kaTuvAgi TiVkisu; vAkapxrXhAra mADu. 
\num{4} (\birx) (\ashi) manasisxna meVle balavAgi -- acocxtutx, muderxyotutx, parxBAva biVru; beraguMTumADu; cakitagoLisu: 
\eng{what knocks me is his impudence} nananxnunx beragugoLisuvudeMdare avana dhASaTxR\kern -3ptyx. 
\num{5} (\birx) (\ashi) peTuTx; saMBoVgisu; jaDi; gumumx. 
\num{6} baDidu, hoDedu (vasutx, vayxkitxyanunx) 

\alnum{a} oLakekx taLuLx, hogisu, dUDu, dabubx:
\eng{knocked the ball into the hole} ceMDanunx kuLiyoLakekx hoDede, kuLiyoLakekx taLiLxde. 

\alnum{b} horakekx, Acege, modalAgi ODisu, aTuTx, dUDu, taLuLx: 
\eng{knocked those ideas out of his head} A BAvanegaLanunx nAnu avana taleyiMda, manasisxniMda 
Acege dUDide, ODiside, aTiTxde.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (oLakekx parxveVshisalu) bAgilu taTuTx; kada baDi: \eng{knock at the door} kada taTuTx. 
\num{2} (moVTAru yA itara eMjinunx) (yAvudoV BAga saDilavAgi yA itara yAMtirxka doVSadiMda) dabadabisu; dabadaba
baDiduko; laTalaTisu; laTalaTa sadudx mADu. 
\num{3} (yaMtarxda eMjininxna \vi) (iMdhana soPxVTada pariNAmavAgi) siDiyutitxru; BAri soPxVTagaLa sadidxna saraNiyanunx sUsu, horabiDu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{knock about (\engit{or} around)} 

\alnum{a} matetx matetx, meVliMda meVle, padeV padeV -- hoDe, baDi, cacucx. 

\alnum{b} (obabxnanunx) oraTAgi, niSuThxravAgi, kaThoVravAgi -- kANu; (obabxna \vi) pirxVti, dayegaLilalxde yA
nidaRyavAgi vatiRsu, naDeduko: \eng{he knocked his children about} avanu tananx
makakxLa bagegx nidaRyavAgi naDedukoLuLxtitxdadx. 

\alnum{c} akasAmxtAtxgi, AkasimxkavAgi--(oMdeDe) iru, hAjariru, upasithxtanAgiru. 

\alnum{d} (kelasavilalxde)
aledADutitxru; sutAtxDutitxru. 

\alnum{e} avayxvasithxta bALanunx baduku; gotutx guriyilalxda jiVvana naDesu. 
\num{2} \eng{knock against} 

\alnum{a} (oMdakekx) baDi; Dikikx hoDe: \eng{the car knocked against a tree} kAru maravoMdakekx baDiyitu, Dikikx hoDeyitu. 

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (obabxnanunx) akasAmxtAtxgi -- kANu, saMdhisu, eduru hAyu: \eng{I knocked against an old crony at the theatre}
nATakashAleyalilx akasAmxtAtxgi nananx haLeya geLeyanobabxnanunx kaMDe.
\num{3} \eng{knock back} (\birx) (\ashi) 

\alnum{a} (\kanmu\ gabagabane) tinunx; mukukx. 

\alnum{b} (\kanmu\ gaTagaTane, beVgabeVga) kuDi. 

\alnum{c} (eNike, yoVjane, kAyaRkarxma, \mo vanunx) keDisu; asatxvayxsatxgoLisu. 

\alnum{d} (AseTxrXVliya matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf) (\AmA) nirAkarisu; dhikakxrisu. 
\num{4} \eng{knock down}

\alnum{a} (vayxkitx, beVTe, shaturx vimAna, \mo vanunx) hoDeduruLisu; hoDedu nelakekx biVLisu: \eng{the hunter knocked the boar down} beVDa kADuhaMdiyanunx hoDeduruLisida. \eng{knocked down by the blazing sun, he died on the spot} uribisilina hoDetadiMda avanu niMtalelxV satutx bidadx. 

\alnum{b} (kaTaTxDa \mo vanunx) keDavu; uruLisu; nelasama mADu. 

\alnum{c} (\rUpa) (vAda \mo vugaLalilx) meVlugeY sAdhisu; maNiyisu; soVlisu. 

\alnum{d} (harAjinalilx sutitxge baDidu) savAludAranige vasutxvanunx -- biDu, koDu, vahisu. 

\alnum{e} (\AmA) (obabxnanunx hADalu) kUgi -- kare, koVru. 

\alnum{f} (\AmA) (vasutxvina) (bele) iLisu; tagigxsu; kaDime mADu. 

\alnum{g} (\ame) (\ashi) kadi; lapaTAyisu; egarisu.

\alnum{h} (vANijayx) (ravAneyalilx jAga uLisalu yaMtarx, piVThoVpakaraNa, \mo vugaLa) BAgagaLanunx -- beVpaRDisu; kaLaci hAku. 

\alnum{i} (AseTxrXVliya matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf) (\ashi) (saMbaLada cekakxnunx, haNavanunx) uDAyisu; KacuR mADi biDu. 
\num{5} \eng{knock off} 

\alnum{a} (tale \mo vanunx) hoDeduruLisu; ETu koTuTx keDavu; hoDedu hAku: \eng{knock person's head off} (obabxna) tale hArisu; tale kaDidu hAku. 

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (obabxnanunx) sulaBavAgi soVlisu; sarAgavAgi miVrisu; sharxmavilalxdaMte tale meTuTx. 

\alnum{c} kelasa mugisade nililxsu, sathxgitagoLisu: \eng{we knocked off at 5.30} nAvu aidUvarege kelasa nililxsidevu, 
sathxgitagoLisidevu. 
\alnum{d} (kelasavanunx) (mADi) mugisu; samApitxgoLisu; konegoLisu; pUNaR mADu: \eng{knocked off work early} beVga kelasa mugisidevu.

\alnum{e} (\AmA) (vayxvahAravanunx) beVgabeVga, avasaravasaravAgi, tavxreyiMda -- mADi mugisu, pUNaRgoLisu. 

\alnum{f} (\AmA) (padayx \mo vanunx) beVga beVga racisu; avasaravasaravAgi heNe, tayArisu. 

\alnum{g} (bele, bilulx, \mo vugaLiMda gotAtxda mobalaganunx) kaDime mADu; kaDidu hAku; vajA mADu. 

\alnum{h} (\ashi) kadi; egarisu; lapaTAyisu. 

\alnum{i} (\birx) (\ashi) (heMgasanunx) keVyu; saMBoVgisu.

\alnum{j} (\ashi) kolulx; koMdu hAku. 
\num{6} \eng{knock on} (ragibx ceMDATadalilx) eduru pakaSxda goVlinatatx (ceMDanunx) keYyiMdaloV, toVLiniMdaloV taLuLx, dUDu, nUku. 

\num{7} \eng{knock out} 

\alnum{a} cuMgANiyanunx (kuTiTx yA taTiTx) -- baridu mADu, KAli mADu; (adaralilxna bUdi, karaku, \mo vanunx) koDavu.

\alnum{b} taleya meVle moTiTx, hoDedu--(obabxnige) parxjecnx tapipxsu, (obabxnanunx) mUCeR hoVgisu. 

\alnum{c} (muSiTxkALagadalilx) (\sA\ hatetxNisuvudaroLagAgi) meVleVLadaMte (malalxnanunx)--hoDedu keDavu; hoDeduruLisu. 

\alnum{d} (\rUpa) (\kanmu\ sapxdhARtamxka paMdayxdalilx) soVlisu. 

\alnum{e} niSapxrXyoVjakagoLisu; nirupayukatxvAgisu; kelasakekx bAradaMte mADu. 

\alnum{f} (\ashi) beragugoLisu; cakitagoLisu; acacxrigoLisu; AshacxyaR huTiTxsu. 

\alnum{g} (\ashi) (\AtAmx) susAtxgu; susutx mADiko; daNidu hoVgu: \eng{knocked themselves out swimming} Iji susutx mADikoMDaru. 

\alnum{h} (\AmA) (yoVjane \mo vanunx) avasaravasaravAgi mADu; avasaradalilx -- racisu, nimiRsu, rUpisu, tayArisu. 

\alnum{i} (AseTxrXVliya matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf, \ame, \ashi)gaLisu; saMpAdisu. 
\num{8} \eng{knock sideways} (\AmA) beragugoLisu; acacxri huTiTxsu. 
\num{9} \eng{knock together} avasaravasaravAgi -- kale hAku, oTiTxge seVrisu: \eng{he knocked together 50 runs}
avanu avasaravasaravAgi $50$ ranunxgaLanunx seVrisida. 
\num{10} \eng{knock under} maNi; sharaNAgu; soVlopipxko; adhiVnanAgu. 
\num{11} \eng{knock up} 

\alnum{a} hoDedu meVlakekx dUDu, taLuLx, Erisu. 

\alnum{b} avasaravasaravAgi mADu yA  EpaRDisu. 

\alnum{c} (kirxkeTf) beVga beVga, kiSxparxvAgi (ranunxgaLanunx)--mADu, gaLisu. 

\alnum{d} (\birx) bAgilu taTiTx, kuTiTx, baDidu (malagiruvavananunx)-- ebibxsu, ecacxragoLisu. 

\alnum{e} susAtxgu; daNidu hoVgu. 

\alnum{f} susAtxgisu; daNisu; susutx mADu. 

\alnum{g} (\ame) (\ashi) basiru mADu; basirAgisu. 

\alnum{h} (ceMDATagaLalilx) paMdayx vidhuyxkatxvAgi shuruvAguvudakikxMta muMce aBAyxsa naDesu, mADu; aBAyxsakAkxgi ceMDanunx alilxMdililxge -- hoDeyutitxru yA odeyutitxru.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{knock into a cocked hat} (yAvudanenxV yA yAranenxV) pUtiR -- soVlisu, miVrisu, jajijx hAku. 
\num{2} \eng{knock into \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{shape(2) pagu(2)}{${}^2$shape}.}  (yAranenxV yA yAvudanenxV) 

\alnum{a} sariyAda rUpakekx taru; utatxma sithxtige taru.

\alnum{b} dashaRniVyavAgisu; aMdavAgi kANuvaMte mADu.

\alnum{c} dakaSxvAgiruvaMte, samathaRvAgiruvaMte -- mADu.
\hyperdef{K}{knock(1) nuga(3)}{}
\num{3} \eng{knock one into the middle of next week} hoDedaTuTx; ododxVDisu. 
\num{4} \eng{knock one's head against} 

\alnum{a} (goVDe \mo vakekx) tale -- baDiduko, tAkisiko. 

\alnum{b} (parxtikUla GaTane, parisithxtigaLoDane) hoVrADu; ahita GaSaRNege baru; tale cacicxko. 
\num{5} \eng{knock on the head} 

\alnum{a} taleya meVle cacicx yA baDidu (vayxkitxyanunx) mUCeR hoVgisu yA kolulx.

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (haMcike, yoVjane, \mo vanunx) tale etatxdaMte mADu; meTuTx; aDagisu; nAshagoLisu.

\bentry
\word[know(1)]{know}
\pron{noV}
\gl{\kirx}
{(\BU\ \eng{knew} \ucAcx\ nUyx; \BUkaq\ \eng{known} \ucAcx\ noVnf).}


\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (yAreMbudanunx, yAvudeMbudanunx) ari; kaMDuko; tiLiduko; gurutisu: \eng{I knew him at once} avanu yAreMbudanunx takaSxNa 
tiLidukoMDe. \eng{I knew him for an Englishman} avanu AMgalxneMbudanunx kaMDukoMDe.
\eng{will you know him again?} avananunx matotxmemx gurutisabalelxyA? 
\num{2} viveVcanAshakitx hoMdiru; (vayxkitxyanunx vayxkitxyiMda, vasutxvanunx vasutxviniMda) beVpaRDisi gurutisu; (avugaLa parasapxra) vayxtAyxsa, tAratamayx, BeVda -- tiLi, ari: \eng{know right from wrong} sarigU tapipxgU naDuvaNa (parasapxra) BeVda tiLi. 
\num{3} (vayxkitx, vasutx, sathxLagaLa) paricaya hoMdiru; (avugaLanunx) tiLidiru, tiLidavanAgiru, balalxvanAgiru: \eng{I know him by sight}
Atananunx keVvala noVDidedxVne aSeTx; nanage avana muKaparicaya ide. \eng{I know him to speak to} Atananunx mAtanADisuvaSuTx balelx. 
\num{4} (Baya, noVvu, \mo vanunx savxMta anuBavadiMda) aritiru; tiLidavanAgiru; balalxvanAgiru. 
\num{5} oLapaTiTxru; oLagAgiru; \eng{her joy knew no bounds} avaLa AnaMdakekx pAraveV iralilalx. 
\num{6} AtimxVyavAgi tiLidiru; nikaTa yA AtimxVya paricaya hoMdiru: \eng{they are our neighbours, but we don't know them} avaru namamx nereyavaru, Adare namage avara 
nikaTa paricaya ilalx. 
\num{7} (\pArxparx) saMBoVgisu; meYthuna naDesu. 
\num{8} tiLidiru; aritiru; tiLidukoMDiru; anuBava yA Odu yA sudidxya PalavAgi (yAvudanenxV) manasisxnalilx yA nenapinalilx iTuTxkoMDiru, hoMdiru: \eng{doesn't know your address} ninanx viLAsa tiLidukoMDilalx, gotitxlalx. \eng{knows a lot about cars} kArugaLa viSaya bahaLa aritidAdxne. \eng{know what to do} Enu mADabeVkeMdu gotitxru. 
\num{9} (saMgatiyoMdara) arivu -- paDediru, hoMdiru; balalxvanAgiru;
gotitxru: \eng{he konws I am waiting} nAnu kAyutitxruvudu avanige arivide; nAnu 
kAyutitxdedxVneMbudu avanige gotitxde. 
\num{10} (BASe, viSaya, \mo vugaLalilx) pAMDitayx hoMdiru; parxButavx paDediru; niSANxtanAgiru; oLeLxya tiLivaLike
hoMdiru; seYdAdhxMtika yA pArxyoVgika jAcnxna hoMdiru. \eng{knows German} 
jamaRnf BASeyanunx cenAnxgi tiLidukoMDidAdxne. \eng{knows his tables}
koVSaTxkagaLalilx niSANxtanAgidAdxne. 
\num{11} KacitavAgi BAvisu; KAtariyAgi
eNisu: \eng{I know it must be somewhere here} adu ilelxV elolxV irabeVkeMdu nanage KacitavAgide.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
{\dictmeaning{tiLidukoMDiru; aritiru.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{all one knows (how)} 

\alnum{a} tiLidadadxnenxlalx. 

\alnum{b} tAnu mADabahudAdadxnenxlalx; tananx shakitxpUtiR. 

\alnum{c} keYlAda maTiTxgU; tananx savaRshakitxyiMdalU AguvaSuTx maTiTxge. 
\num{2} \eng{before one knows where one is} digaBxrXmegoLisuvaSuTx shiVGarxvAgi; kaMgeDisuvaSuTx kiSxparxvAgi; kakAkxbikikx 
mADuvaSuTx beVga. 
\num{3} \eng{be not to know} 

\alnum{a} yAvudeV riVtiyalilx tiLiyalAgadaMtiru; tiLidukoLuLxva -- mAgaR, vidhAna, rahA ilalxdiru: \eng{wasn't to know they'd arrive late} avaru taDavAgi barutAtxreMdu tiLidukoLaLxlAgalilalx. 

\alnum{b} (obabxnige) heVLakUDadaMtiru; tiLisabAradaMtiru: \eng{she's not to know about the party} saMtoVSakUTada viSaya avaLige
tiLisabAradu. 
\num{4} \eng{don't I know it?} (\AmA) (viSAdadiMda opipxkoLuLxva, samamxtisuva mAtAgi) nanage gotitxlalxveV? nanage tiLiyadeV? (gotitxde, manasisxlalxdidadxrU opipxkoLaLxbeVkAgide eMbathaRdalilx). 
\num{5} \eng{don't you know?} (mAtina naDuve seVrisuva nirathaRka padagucaCxvAgi) ninage gotitxlalxveV?
ninage tiLiyadeV?: \eng{It is such a bore, don't you know?} adoMdu shudadhx
beVjArina saMgati, ninage gotitxlalxveV? 
\num{6} \eng{for all (\engit{or} aught) I know} nanage tiLidiruva maTiTxge; nananx arivige saMbaMdhisiruva maTiTxge. 
\num{7} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{god(1) pagu(12)}{${}^1$god}
\engit{or} \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{heaven pagu(6)}{heaven}
\engit{or} the \hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{Lord(1) pagu(14)}{${}^1$lord} (only) knows} 

\alnum{a} (nananx yA matayxRmAnavana arivige, manuSayxna arivige miVridudx eMbudanunx sUcisalu heVLuva mAtu) deVvarobabxnige
gotutx; BagavaMta mAtarx balalx.

\alnum{b} nananx heVLikege deVvareV sAkiSx; deVvara sAkiSxyAgi nAnu heVLuvudeVneMdare.
\num{8} \eng{has been known to do} mADutAtxneMdu gotAtxgide, parxsidadhxvAgide:
\eng{he has been known to be unreliable} avanu vishAvxsAhaRnalalx eMbudu gotAtxgide. 
\num{9} \eng{I knew it} nanage adu gotitxtutx. adu AgiyeV AgutatxdeMdu
nanage KAtariyAgitutx, KacitavAgi tiLiditutx. 
\num{10} \eng{I know what} EneMbudu nanage gotutx; muMdiDalu yA maMDisalu nananxlilx, nananx hatitxra, nananx baLi oMdu hosa kalapxne, aBipArxya yA sUcane uMTu, ide. 
\num{11} \eng{know about} (oMdara, obabxna) viSayavanunx tiLidiru; samAcAra aritiru.
\num{12} \eng{know a \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{hawk(1) nuga}{${}^1$hawk} from a handsaw} sAmAnayx parijAcnxna paDediru; (loVka) vayxvahArajAcnxna hoMdiru; sAmAnayx viveVcane iru.
\num{13} \eng{know a thing or two}

\alnum{a} anuBava paDediru; anuBaviyAgiru. 

\alnum{b} curukubudidhxyavanAgiru; sUkaSxmX parijAcnxna hoMdiru. 
\num{14} \eng{know best} itararigiMta hecucx tiLidavanu \mo vanu Agiru yA hAge heVLiko. 
\num{15} \eng{know better (than that)} adakikxMta hecucx gotitxru; adanunx naMbadiruvaSuTx, aMte naDedukoLaLxdiruvaSuTx tiLidukoMDiru. 
\num{16} \eng{know better than to do} hAge mADuvaSuTx daDaDxnalalx yA asaMsakxqqtanalalx, ayoVgayxnalalx. 
\hyperdef{K}{know(1) nuga(17)}{}
\num{17} \eng{know by sight}

\alnum{a} cahareyiMda, noVTadiMda, noVDuvudariMda (mAtarx)--gurutisu, tiLi.

\alnum{b} noVDi aSeTxV iru; noVDi mAtarx paricayaviru. 
\num{18} \eng{know how} (yAvudanenxV) mADuva vidhAnavanunx tiLidiru. 
\num{19} \eng{known as} A hesarina; A hesaru uLaLx, paDeda. 
\num{20} \eng{know of} gotitxru; tiLidiru; keVLiru: \eng{not that I know of} nanage tiLida maTiTxge ilalx, alalx.
\num{21} \eng{know (one) by name} 

\alnum{a} hesariniMdaSeTxV balelx; hesaranunx mAtarx keVLi balelx; hesaraSeTxV gotutx. 

\alnum{b} (obabxna, oMdara) hesaru gotutx; hesaru tiLisabalelx, heVLabalelx. 
\num{22} \eng{know one's own mind} sithxra saMkalapx uLaLxvanAgiru; daqDhamanasusxLaLxvanAgiru; sithxrabudidhxyuLaLxvanAgiru; daqDhacitatxnAgiru; caMcalacitatxnAgadiru; manasusx OlADadiru; nishicxtasaMkalapxvuLaLxvanAgiru. 
\num{23} \eng{know one's way round} 

\alnum{a} (sathxLa, viSaya, kAyaRkarxma, \mo vugaLa) paricaya paDediru; (avanunx) sariyAgi, cenAnxgi tiLidukoMDiru. 

\alnum{b} cenAnxgi tiLidukoMDavanU dakaSxnU Agiru. 
\num{24} \eng{know (person or thing) to be} (vayxkitx yA vasutxvanunx) hAgeMdu, aMteMdu -- ari, tiLi: \eng{know him to be learned} Ata vidAvxMsaneMbudanunx tiLidiru. 
\num{25} \eng{know (person or thing) to do} (vayxkitx yA vasutx) hAge, aMte -- mADutAtxne yA mADutatxde eMbudanunx tiLidiru, aritiru. 
\num{26} \eng{know the ropes (\engit{or} one's stuff)} yAvudAdarU oMdu kAyaRkeSxVtarxda parisithxtiyanunx, vidayxmAnagaLanunx tiLidiru;
(keYkoMDa kelasada yA viSayada) vivaragaLa yA vidayxmAnagaLa pUNaR paricaya hoMdiru; oMdu kelasa mADuva riVtiyanunx tiLidiru. 
\num{27} \eng{know what one is talking about}
(\AmA) Enu mAtanADutitxdedxVye, heVLutitxdidxVye eMbudanunx tiLidiru; anuBavadiMda yA anuBavaviruva viSayavanunx mAtarx kuritu mAtanADu. 
\hyperdef{K}{know(1) nuga(28)}{}
\num{28} \eng{know what's what} loVkAnuBava hoMdiru; vayxvahAra jAcnxnaviru; Enu, etatx enunxvudanunx tiLidiru; parxpaMcada vasutx matutx vayxvahAragaLa bagegx sariyAda yA sAkaSuTx sAmAnayx jAcnxna hoMdiru; yAvudu Enu eMbudanunx aritiru. 
\num{29} \eng{know who's who} parxtiyobabx vayxkitxyU yAru Enu eMbudanunx aritiru, tiLidiru.
\num{30} \eng{let it be known} tiLiyuvaMtAgali; tiLiyapaDisali; parxkaTisali. 
\num{31} \eng{let me know} nanage -- tiLisu, tiLiyapaDisu, tiLiyaheVLu, tiLiyuvaMte mADu. 
\num{32} \eng{make oneself known to somebody} yAroV obabxrige tananx
paricaya mADisiko. 
\num{33} \eng{not if I know it} nananx iceCxge, saMkalapxkekx virudadhxvAgi mAtarx. 
\num{34} \eng{not know any better} (sariyAda shikaSxNa, anuBava, \mo vu ilalxda kAraNa) sariyAgi, saBayxvAgi -- vatiRsadiru. 
\num{35} \eng{not know(one) from \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{adam(1) nuga(1)}{${}^1$adam}} nanage avana guruteV ilalx; avanu heVgidAdxneMbudeV nanage  tiLiyadu.
\num{36} \eng{not know that...} (\AmA) KacitavAgilalxdiru; sAkaSuTx daqDhavAgilalxdiru:
\eng{I don't know that I want to go} hoVgabeVkeniside eMdu nanage KacitavAgilalx. 
\num{37} \eng{not know that hit one} 

\alnum{a} idadxkikxdadxMte hatanAgu;
haThAtAtxgi kolalxlapxDu; idadxkikxdadxMte koleyAgu. 

\alnum{b} pUtiR
digaBxrXmegoLuLx; kakAkxbikikxyAgu. 
\num{38} \eng{not want to know} (oMdakekx)
gamana -- koDadiru, harisadiru; tiLiyalu iciCxsadiru; ariyalu iSaTxpaDadiru.
\num{39} \eng{that's all you know (about that)} ninage (adara bagegx) gotitxruvudelalx aSeTxV; niVnu aMdukoMDiruvudakikxMtalU hecucx daDaDx, BAvisikoMDiruvudakikxMtalU hecucx ajacnx. 
\num{40} \eng{ what do you know (about that)?} (\AmA\ AshacxyaRsUcakavAgi)
ninage (adara bagegx) Enu gotutx, Enu tiLidide? 
\num{41} \eng{you know} (\AmA) (keVLuganige A viSaya gotutx yA avanu adanunx tiLidukoLaLxbeVkAgitutx eMbudanunx nenapu mADalu yA saMBASaNeya naDuvaNa terapanunx tuMbuva mAtAgi baLasuva)
ninage, ninageV yA ninagU -- gotutx, tiLidide. 
\num{42} \eng{you know something (\engit{or} what)?} nAnu ninage oMdu viSaya heVLalidedxVne. 
\num{43} \eng{you know what he \engit{or} it is} avanu yA adu Enu enunxvudu ninage gotutx; ninage avana yA adara guNAvaguNagaLu, jaTila savxBAva, savxrUpa, \mo vu gotutx,
avugaLa paricayavide. 
\num{44} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_y.pdf}{Y}{you pagu(3)}{you} know-what (\engit{or}-who)} (yArU, yAvudu eMdu niSakxqqSaTxvAgi heVLade adhAyxhAravAgiruvalilx) `ninage gotatxlalx, 
yArU (yA yAvudu) aMta?'
\num{45} \eng{you never know} muMdeVnu enunxvudu KacitavAgi gotAtxgadu; BaviSayx anishicxta; nALeyadu pUtiR KAtariyAgi tiLiyuvudilalx.}}
\eentry
